 492 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/kernel/kernel.py`
 493 | **Components & Logic:**
 494 | 
 495 | - ðŸ“¦ **`Kernel`**
 496 |     > *The Event Publisher.*
 497 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`__init__`**
 498 |       * Stateless singleton pattern
 499 | 
 500 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`publish`**
 501 |       > *Ingests an event into the System Outbox.*
 502 |       * **1.** RESOLVE METADATA
 503 |       * **2.** RESOLVE CONTEXT
 504 |       * We grab the Trace ID from the request context to link API logs with Kafka logs
 505 |       * **3.** RESOLVE PARTITION KEY (Critical for Kafka)
 506 |       * If not provided, we try to use entity_id. If that's missing, we fallback to "global".
 507 |       * **WARNING:** "global" puts everything on one partition (ordering guaranteed but low throughput).
 508 |       * **4.** ENVELOPE CONSTRUCTION
 509 |       * **5.** WRITE TO OUTBOX
 510 |       * In Level 100, we DO raise. If the event cannot be logged, the transaction is unsafe.
 511 | 
 512 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`commit`**
 513 |       > *Finalizes the transaction.*
 514 |

 779 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/meta/engine.py`
 780 | **Components & Logic:**
 781 | 
 782 | - ðŸ“¦ **`PolicyEngine`**
 783 |     > *The Universal Logic Executor.*
 784 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`evaluate`**
 785 |       > *The Main Entry Point.*
 786 |       * **1.** Prepare Data Context (Sandbox Envelope)
 787 |       * We wrap the data to allow 'context.meta' or 'context.actor' access if needed later.
 788 |       * Strategy: Pass object directly. Rules should be written as `host.weight > 10`.
 789 |       * **2.** Iterate Policies
 790 |       * **3.** Merge Results based on Governance Strategy
 791 |       * **4.** Apply Resolution Strategy ( The Judge )
 792 | 
 793 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_evaluate_single_policy`**
 794 |       > *Executes one Policy Bundle (which may contain multiple Rules).*
 795 |       * Policies store rules as a JSONB list: [{ "logic": "...", "action": "BLOCK", ... }]
 796 |       * A. Execute JMESPath
 797 |       * Boolean expressions: `host.age > 18` returns True/False.
 798 |       * B. Handle Match (Triggered)
 799 |       * âš¡ RESOLVE DYNAMIC VALUES
 800 |       * If action involves data, we must check if the value is a reference (e.g. actor.id)
 801 |       * **SAFEGUARD:** Bad rule syntax should not crash the system.
 802 |       * âš¡ FAIL OPEN: Treat crash as WARNING, not BLOCK.
 803 | 
 804 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_resolve_value`**
 805 |       > *Detects if a value is a reference (e.g. 'actor.id') and resolves it against the context.*
 806 |       * Heuristic: If it looks like a known context path, try to resolve it.
 807 |       * This matches the 'Value Source' logic in the Frontend Policy Editor.
 808 |       * If resolution works, return it. If it returns None, it might mean the field is missing,
 809 |       * but we return None rather than the string literal "actor.id".
 810 |       * If JMESPath crashes, fallback to the string literal
 811 | 
 812 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_apply_strategy`**
 813 |       > *Decides the final outcome based on the strategy.*
 814 |       * Default: Any violation kills the transaction
 815 |       * If (Total - Violations) > 0, then Pass.
 816 | 
 817 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_serialize`**
 818 |       > *Helper to convert SQLAlchemy objects to Dict for JMESPath.*
 819 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_log_summary`**
 820 |

 863 | - ðŸ“¦ **`XStateInterpreter`**
 864 |     > *A lightweight, fault-tolerant interpreter for XState v5 definitions.*
 865 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`__init__`**
 866 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`get_initial_state`**
 867 |       > *Returns the starting state of the machine.*

 869 |       > *Determines the next state based on the current state and the incoming event.*
 870 |       * **1.** Validate Current State
 871 |       * **2.** Look for Transitions ('on' block)
 872 |       * **3.** Match Event
 873 |       * XState allows 'on': { "EVENT": "TARGET" } OR 'on': { "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET" } }
 874 |       * **4.** Resolve Target
 875 |       * Short syntax: "EVENT": "TARGET"
 876 |       * Object syntax: "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET", "actions": [...] }
 877 |       * Array syntax (Guards): "EVENT": [{ "target": "T1", "guard": "cond" }]
 878 |       * For Phase 1, we just take the first unconditional match or the first one.
 879 |       * **TODO:** Implement Guard Logic evaluation here.

1332 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utilities/async_bridge.py`
1333 | **Components & Logic:**
1334 | 
1335 | - ðŸ“¦ **`AsyncBridge`**
1336 |     > *The Connector between the Blocking DB Layer and the Non-Blocking Logic Layer.*
1337 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`run_sync`**
1338 |       > *Executes a coroutine synchronously by spawning a fresh Event Loop in a separate thread.*
1339 |       * âš¡ 1. CAPTURE CONTEXT
1340 |       * Snapshot the current state (User, Request ID, etc.)
1341 |       * This allows the background thread to "know" who initiated the save.
1342 |       * âš¡ 2. SETUP SIDECAR LOOP
1343 |       * âš¡ 3. EXECUTE WITHIN CONTEXT
1344 |       * We wrap the execution in ctx.run() so the coroutine sees the vars.
1345 |       * Note: We must wrap the loop.run_until_complete call itself,
1346 |       * or create a wrapper task that runs in context.
1347 |       * Best practice: ctx.run(task)
1348 |       * The loop itself doesn't need the context, the coroutine does.
1349 |       * However, ctx.run() takes a callable.
1350 |       * We simply run the loop logic.
1351 |       * This ensures the async task inherits the context
1352 |       * But simpler: we just run the whole block in context if possible.
1353 |       * Actually, contextvars context applies to the *thread* execution stack.
1354 |       * So executing ctx.run(func) sets the context for 'func'.
1355 |       * âš¡ 4. SPAWN THREAD WITH CONTEXT
1356 |       * We pass 'target' to ctx.run, so 'target' runs with the variables set.
1357 |       * But we are starting a NEW thread. ctx.run() only works in the CURRENT thread.
1358 |       * To pass context to a NEW thread, we must run ctx.run INSIDE the new thread.
1359 |       * "Re-hydrate" the context inside the new thread
1360 |       * Block until the Sidecar finishes (Gatekeeper behavior)
1361 | 
1362 | 
1363 | ---
1364 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utils/reflection.py`
1365 | **Components & Logic:**
1366 | 
1367 | - Æ’ **`reflect_model_schema`**
1368 |     > *Introspects a SQLAlchemy Model and returns a structured Context Graph.*
1369 |     * Indentation for logging readability
1370 |     * **1.** SCALAR FIELDS
1371 |     * âš¡ ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: Skip Dynamic Containers
1372 |     * The bucket itself is not a field, it holds the fields.
1373 |     * --- A. Type Mapping ---
1374 |     * Map SQLAlchemy Types to UI Types
1375 |     * --- B. Metadata Extraction (The Explicit Strategy) ---
1376 |     * We look for the 'info' dict on the column definition first.
1377 |     * Fallback to Heuristics if missing.
1378 |     * Label: Override or Auto-Generate
1379 |     * System/Read-Only Status
1380 |     * **1.** Explicit Override
1381 |     * **2.** Heuristic Fallback (Safety Net)
1382 |     * Final Decision Logic
1383 |     * Special Case: 'hashed_password'
1384 |     * Should be "password" widget, but never readable.
1385 |     * --- C. Construct Field Definition ---
1386 |     * Alias for logic engine
1387 |     * Placeholder for extended config
1388 |     * Inject options if found via Enum or Info
1389 |     * **2.** RELATIONSHIPS (The Graph)
1390 |     * Only recurse if we haven't hit the limit
1391 |     * Determine Cardinality
1392 |     * Recursive Call
1393 |     * **3.** CONSTRUCT OUTPUT

2033 |     * --- RESET MODE (Reverse Waves) ---
2034 |     * âš¡ PHASE 0.5: KERNEL HYDRATION
2035 |     * --- SEED MODE (Forward Waves) ---
2036 |     * Guard: Don't run History in Prod unless explicit
2037 | 
2038 | - Æ’ **`main`**
2039 | 
2040 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/trigger_circuit.py`
2041 | **Components & Logic:**
2042 | 
2043 | - Æ’ **`fire_circuit_event`**
2044 |     * âš¡ MANUALLY REGISTER INTERCEPTOR (Required for standalone scripts)
2045 |     * **1.** Ensure it exists (Prime the cache/db)
2046 |     * **2.** Toggle State (The Mutation)
2047 |     * This calls the refactored ORM method
2048 |     * **3.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor)
2049 | 
2050 | 
2051 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/trigger_event.py`
2052 | **Components & Logic:**
2053 | 
2054 | - Æ’ **`fire_test_event`**
2055 |     * **âš¡ CRITICAL:** We must register the interceptor manually for this script context
2056 |     * In the real app, main.py does this.
2057 |     * **1.** Fetch User
2058 |     * **2.** Modify State (Trigger Dirty Check)
2059 |     * We update a field to force SQLAlchemy to mark it 'dirty'
2060 |     * **3.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor -> Outbox)
2061 | 
2062 | 
2063 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/trigger_meta.py`
2064 | **Components & Logic:**
2065 | 
2066 | - Æ’ **`fire_meta_event`**
2067 |     * Register Interceptor
2068 |     * Verify Registration
2069 |     * **1.** Create Policy
2070 |     * **2.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor)

# Source code from: frontend\src\_kernel\CapabilitiesContext.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | /* FILEPATH: frontend/src/_kernel/CapabilitiesContext.tsx */
   2 | /* @file Capabilities Provider (The Hydrator) */
   3 | /* @author The Engineer */
   4 | /* @description Blocks app rendering until the System Registry is synced.
   5 |  * MIGRATION: Swapped Material UI for Ant Design v5.
   6 |  */
   7 | 
   8 | import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
   9 | import { Spin, Typography, theme, Flex } from 'antd';
  10 | import { LoadingOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
  11 | 
  12 | // Types
  13 | import { SystemRegistry } from './SystemRegistry';
  14 | 
  15 | // The Context Interface
  16 | interface CapabilitiesContextType {
  17 |   isReady: boolean;
  18 |   registry: typeof SystemRegistry;
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | const CapabilitiesContext = createContext<CapabilitiesContextType | null>(null);
  22 | 
  23 | export const CapabilitiesProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  24 |   const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
  25 |   const { token } = theme.useToken();
  26 | 
  27 |   useEffect(() => {
  28 |     const boot = async () => {
  29 |       // Execute the Handshake
  30 |       await SystemRegistry.initialize();
  31 |       setIsReady(true);
  32 |     };
  33 |     boot();
  34 |   }, []);
  35 | 
  36 |   if (!isReady) {
  37 |     return (
  38 |       <Flex 
  39 |         vertical 
  40 |         align="center" 
  41 |         justify="center" 
  42 |         style={{ 
  43 |           height: '100vh', 
  44 |           backgroundColor: '#0a0a0a', // Deep dark
  45 |           color: '#ffffff',
  46 |           gap: 16 
  47 |         }}
  48 |       >
  49 |         <Spin indicator={<LoadingOutlined style={{ fontSize: 48, color: token.colorPrimary }} spin />} />
  50 |         
  51 |         <Typography.Text style={{ fontFamily: 'monospace', opacity: 0.8, color: token.colorPrimary }}>
  52 |           INITIALIZING KERNEL LINK...
  53 |         </Typography.Text>
  54 |         
  55 |         <Typography.Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: 12 }}>
  56 |           Fetching System Capabilities
  57 |         </Typography.Text>
  58 |       </Flex>
  59 |     );
  60 |   }
  61 | 
  62 |   return (
  63 |     <CapabilitiesContext.Provider value={{ isReady, registry: SystemRegistry }}>
  64 |       {children}
  65 |     </CapabilitiesContext.Provider>
  66 |   );
  67 | };
  68 | 
  69 | // Hook for consuming the capabilities
  70 | export const useCapabilities = () => {
  71 |   const context = useContext(CapabilitiesContext);
  72 |   if (!context) {
  73 |     throw new Error("useCapabilities must be used within a CapabilitiesProvider");
  74 |   }
  75 |   return context.registry;
  76 | };
  77 |

   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta_v2/features/governance/components/editor/ConsequenceStack.tsx
   2 | // @file: Consequence Stack Manager
   3 | // @role: ðŸŽ¨ UI Presentation / ðŸ§  Logic Container */
   4 | // @author: The Engineer
   5 | // @description: Renders the action stack for a rule. Driven by dynamic Backend Capabilities (Dumb UI Pattern).
   6 | // @security-level: LEVEL 9 (UI Safe) */
   7 | 
   8 | import React from 'react';
   9 | import { Button, Select, Input, Typography, Space, theme, Empty } from 'antd';
  10 | import { PlusOutlined, DeleteOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
  11 | 
  12 | import { logger } from '@/platform/logging/Narrator';
  13 | import { IconFactory } from '@/platform/ui/icons/IconFactory';
  14 | import { useCapabilities } from '@/_kernel/CapabilitiesContext';
  15 | 
  16 | import type { Consequence, SchemaField } from '../../../../../meta/features/governance/types';
  17 | 
  18 | const { Text } = Typography;
  19 | const { Option, OptGroup } = Select;
  20 | 
  21 | interface ConsequenceStackProps {
  22 |     ruleIdx: number;
  23 |     consequences: Consequence[];
  24 |     schemaFields: SchemaField[];
  25 |     onAdd: (ruleIdx: number) => void;
  26 |     onRemove: (ruleIdx: number, consIdx: number) => void;
  27 |     onUpdate: (ruleIdx: number, consIdx: number, field: string, val: any) => void;
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | export const ConsequenceStack: React.FC<ConsequenceStackProps> = ({
  31 |     ruleIdx, consequences, schemaFields, onAdd, onRemove, onUpdate
  32 | }) => {
  33 |     const { token } = theme.useToken();
  34 |     
  35 |     // âš¡ THE DUMB UI LINK: Read Actions directly from the Kernel's Context Schema
  36 |     const { capabilities } = useCapabilities();
  37 |     const actions = capabilities?.actions || [];
  38 | 
  39 |     // Derived options for target fields
  40 |     const hostFields = schemaFields.filter(f => f.group === 'HOST');
  41 | 
  42 |     return (
  43 |         <div style={{ background: token.colorFillAlter, padding: 12, borderRadius: '0 0 8px 8px', border: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`, borderTop: 'none' }}>
  44 |             <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 8 }}>
  45 |                 <Text strong style={{ fontSize: 12, color: token.colorTextSecondary }}>CONSEQUENCES (EXECUTED IN ORDER)</Text>
  46 |                 <Button type="dashed" size="small" icon={<PlusOutlined />} onClick={() => onAdd(ruleIdx)}>Add Effect</Button>
  47 |             </div>
  48 | 
  49 |             {(!consequences || consequences.length === 0) ? (
  50 |                 <Empty image={Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE} description="No consequences defined. This rule does nothing." style={{ margin: '8px 0' }} />
  51 |             ) : (
  52 |                 <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>
  53 |                     {consequences.map((cons, cIdx) => (
  54 |                         <div key={cons.id} style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, alignItems: 'center', background: token.colorBgContainer, padding: 8, borderRadius: 4, border: `1px solid ${token.colorBorder}` }}>
  55 |                             
  56 |                             {/* âš¡ DYNAMIC CAPABILITIES SELECTOR */}
  57 |                             <Select 
  58 |                                 value={cons.type} 
  59 |                                 style={{ width: 220 }} 
  60 |                                 onChange={v => {
  61 |                                     logger.trace("UI", `Changed consequence type to ${v}`, { ruleIdx, cIdx });
  62 |                                     onUpdate(ruleIdx, cIdx, 'type', v);
  63 |                                 }}
  64 |                                 dropdownMatchSelectWidth={false}
  65 |                             >
  66 |                                 {actions.map((group: any) => (
  67 |                                     <OptGroup label={group.label} key={group.label}>
  68 |                                         {group.options.map((opt: any) => (
  69 |                                             <Option value={opt.value} key={opt.value}>
  70 |                                                 <Space>
  71 |                                                     <IconFactory icon={opt.icon} style={{ color: opt.color }} />
  72 |                                                     {opt.label}
  73 |                                                 </Space>
  74 |                                             </Option>
  75 |                                         ))}
  76 |                                     </OptGroup>
  77 |                                 ))}
  78 |                             </Select>
  79 | 
  80 |                             {/* DYNAMIC PARAMS */}
  81 |                             <div style={{ flex: 1, display: 'flex', gap: 8 }}>
  82 |                                 {/* MESSAGE */}
  83 |                                 {['BLOCK', 'WARN', 'REQUIRE'].includes(cons.type) && (
  84 |                                     <Input 
  85 |                                         placeholder="Message to user..." 
  86 |                                         value={cons.params?.message} 
  87 |                                         onChange={e => onUpdate(ruleIdx, cIdx, 'params.message', e.target.value)} 
  88 |                                     />
  89 |                                 )}
  90 | 
  91 |                                 {/* TARGET FIELD */}
  92 |                                 {['SET_VALUE', 'HIDE', 'SHOW', 'DISABLE', 'ENABLE', 'REQUIRE'].includes(cons.type) && (
  93 |                                     <Select 
  94 |                                         placeholder="Target Field"
  95 |                                         style={{ minWidth: 150 }}
  96 |                                         showSearch
  97 |                                         value={cons.params?.target_field}
  98 |                                         onChange={v => onUpdate(ruleIdx, cIdx, 'params.target_field', v)}
  99 |                                     >
 100 |                                         {hostFields.map(f => (
 101 |                                             <Option key={f.key} value={f.key.replace('host.', '')}>{f.label}</Option>
 102 |                                         ))}
 103 |                                     </Select>
 104 |                                 )}
 105 | 
 106 |                                 {/* VALUE */}
 107 |                                 {cons.type === 'SET_VALUE' && (
 108 |                                     <Input 
 109 |                                         placeholder="Value" 
 110 |                                         value={cons.params?.value} 
 111 |                                         onChange={e => onUpdate(ruleIdx, cIdx, 'params.value', e.target.value)} 
 112 |                                     />
 113 |                                 )}
 114 | 
 115 |                                 {/* EVENT */}
 116 |                                 {cons.type === 'TRIGGER_EVENT' && (
 117 |                                     <Input 
 118 |                                         placeholder="Event Key (e.g. USER:RISK)" 
 119 |                                         value={cons.params?.event_key} 
 120 |                                         onChange={e => onUpdate(ruleIdx, cIdx, 'params.event_key', e.target.value)} 
 121 |                                     />
 122 |                                 )}
 123 |                             </div>
 124 | 
 125 |                             <Button type="text" danger icon={<DeleteOutlined />} onClick={() => onRemove(ruleIdx, cIdx)} />
 126 |                         </div>
 127 |                     ))}
 128 |                 </div>
 129 |             )}
 130 |         </div>
 131 |     );
 132 | };

   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta_v2/features/governance/components/editor/PolicyEditor.tsx

   7 | 
   8 | import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
   9 | import { Form, Input, Button, Card, Row, Col, Typography, theme, Space, Divider, Switch, Tag, Tooltip } from 'antd';
  10 | import { DeleteOutlined, SafetyCertificateOutlined, HistoryOutlined, CloudUploadOutlined, FileTextOutlined, PlusOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
  11 | 
  12 | import { logger } from '@/platform/logging/Narrator';
  13 | import { useUrlState } from '@/platform/hooks/useUrlState';
  14 | 
  15 | // âš¡ V2 HOOKS & COMPONENTS
  16 | import { useGovernance } from '../../hooks/useGovernance';
  17 | import { ConsequenceStack } from './ConsequenceStack';
  18 | 
  19 | // âš¡ V1 IMPORTS (Pending Migration to V2 for Batch 3)
  20 | import { LogicBuilder } from '../../../../../meta/features/governance/components/editor/LogicBuilder';
  21 | import { TestPanel } from '../../../../../meta/features/governance/components/editor/TestPanel';
  22 | import { HistoryDrawer } from '../../../../../meta/features/governance/components/editor/HistoryDrawer';
  23 | 
  24 | import type { PolicyDraft, Rule, Consequence } from '../../../../../meta/features/governance/types';
  25 | 
  26 | const { TextArea } = Input;
  27 | const { Title, Text } = Typography;
  28 | 
  29 | interface PolicyEditorProps {
  30 |     draft: PolicyDraft;
  31 |     domain: string;
  32 |     onSave: (policy: PolicyDraft) => void;
  33 |     onDelete?: () => void;
  34 |     isSaving: boolean;
  35 | }
  36 | 
  37 | export const PolicyEditor: React.FC<PolicyEditorProps> = ({
  38 |     draft: initialDraft,
  39 |     domain,
  40 |     onSave,
  41 |     onDelete,
  42 |     isSaving
  43 | }) => {
  44 |     const { token } = theme.useToken();
  45 |     const [form] = Form.useForm();
  46 |     
  47 |     // âš¡ HYDRATED DATA SOURCE
  48 |     const { schemaContext, loadingSchema } = useGovernance(domain);
  49 |     const schemaFields = schemaContext?.fields || [];
  50 | 
  51 |     const [localDraft, setLocalDraft] = useState<PolicyDraft>(initialDraft);
  52 |     
  53 |     // âš¡ DEEP LINKING BY DEFAULT (Cures History Drawer Amnesia)
  54 |     const [historyMode, setHistoryMode] = useUrlState('history', '');
  55 | 
  56 |     useEffect(() => {
  57 |         setLocalDraft(initialDraft);
  58 |         form.setFieldsValue(initialDraft);
  59 |     }, [initialDraft.key, initialDraft.id, form]);
  60 | 
  61 |     // --- HANDLERS ---
  62 | 
  63 |     const handleNameChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
  64 |         const newName = e.target.value;
  65 |         setLocalDraft(prev => {
  66 |             const updates: Partial<PolicyDraft> = { name: newName };
  67 |             if (!prev.id) {
  68 |                 updates.key = newName.toLowerCase()
  69 |                     .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '_')
  70 |                     .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, '');
  71 |             }
  72 |             return { ...prev, ...updates } as PolicyDraft;
  73 |         });
  74 |     };
  75 | 
  76 |     const handleLogicChange = (idx: number, val: string) => {
  77 |         const rules = [...localDraft.rules];
  78 |         if (rules[idx]) {
  79 |             rules[idx] = { ...rules[idx], logic: val };
  80 |             setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, rules }));
  81 |         }
  82 |     };
  83 | 
  84 |     const addConsequence = (ruleIdx: number) => {
  85 |         const rules = [...localDraft.rules];
  86 |         const newConsequence: Consequence = {
  87 |             id: `cons_${Date.now()}`,
  88 |             type: 'BLOCK' as any, // Default fallback
  89 |             params: { message: "Validation Failed" }
  90 |         };
  91 |         rules[ruleIdx].consequences = [...(rules[ruleIdx].consequences || []), newConsequence];
  92 |         setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, rules }));
  93 |     };
  94 | 
  95 |     const removeConsequence = (ruleIdx: number, consIdx: number) => {
  96 |         const rules = [...localDraft.rules];
  97 |         const cons = [...(rules[ruleIdx].consequences || [])];
  98 |         cons.splice(consIdx, 1);
  99 |         rules[ruleIdx].consequences = cons;
 100 |         setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, rules }));
 101 |     };
 102 | 
 103 |     const updateConsequence = (ruleIdx: number, consIdx: number, field: string, val: any) => {
 104 |         const rules = [...localDraft.rules];
 105 |         const cons = [...rules[ruleIdx].consequences];
 106 |         
 107 |         if (field === 'type') {
 108 |             cons[consIdx] = { ...cons[consIdx], type: val, params: {} };
 109 |         } else if (field.startsWith('params.')) {
 110 |             const paramKey = field.split('.')[1];
 111 |             cons[consIdx] = { 
 112 |                 ...cons[consIdx], 
 113 |                 params: { ...cons[consIdx].params, [paramKey]: val } 
 114 |             };
 115 |         }
 116 |         rules[ruleIdx].consequences = cons;
 117 |         setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, rules }));
 118 |     };
 119 | 
 120 |     const addRule = () => {
 121 |         const newRule: Rule = {
 122 |             id: `rule_${Date.now()}`,
 123 |             logic: "",
 124 |             consequences: [],
 125 |             is_active: true
 126 |         };
 127 |         setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, rules: [...p.rules, newRule] }));
 128 |         logger.tell("UI", "âž• Added new Logic Rule block");
 129 |     };
 130 | 
 131 |     const deleteRule = (idx: number) => {
 132 |         const rules = localDraft.rules.filter((_, i) => i !== idx);
 133 |         setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, rules }));
 134 |     };
 135 | 
 136 |     const handleDualSave = (asActive: boolean) => {
 137 |         onSave({ ...localDraft, is_active: asActive });
 138 |     };
 139 | 
 140 |     const versionDisplay = localDraft.id 
 141 |         // @ts-ignore
 142 |         ? `v${localDraft.version_major || 1}.${(localDraft.version_minor || 0).toString().padStart(2, '0')}`
 143 |         : 'New';
 144 | 
 145 |     return (
 146 |         <div style={{ maxWidth: 1000, margin: '0 auto', paddingBottom: 48 }}>
 147 |             {/* HEADER & METADATA CARD */}
 148 |             <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 24 }}>
 149 |                 <Space align="start">
 150 |                     <SafetyCertificateOutlined style={{ fontSize: 24, color: token.colorPrimary, marginTop: 4 }} />
 151 |                     <div>
 152 |                         <Space>
 153 |                             <Title level={3} style={{ margin: 0 }}>{localDraft.name || 'New Policy'}</Title>
 154 |                             {localDraft.id && (
 155 |                                 <Tag color={localDraft.is_active ? "green" : "gold"}>
 156 |                                     {localDraft.is_active ? versionDisplay : `${versionDisplay} (DRAFT)`}
 157 |                                 </Tag>
 158 |                             )}
 159 |                         </Space>
 160 |                         <div style={{ marginTop: 4 }}>
 161 |                             <Text type="secondary">{localDraft.key || 'System Key: <Auto-Generated>'}</Text>
 162 |                             {domain === 'GLOBAL' && <Tag color="purple" style={{ marginLeft: 8 }}>GLOBAL SCOPE</Tag>}
 163 |                         </div>
 164 |                     </div>
 165 |                 </Space>
 166 |                 <Space>
 167 |                     {localDraft.id && <Button icon={<HistoryOutlined />} onClick={() => setHistoryMode('open')}>History</Button>}
 168 |                     <Tooltip title="Save Draft"><Button icon={<FileTextOutlined />} loading={isSaving} onClick={() => handleDualSave(false)}>Draft</Button></Tooltip>
 169 |                     <Tooltip title="Publish"><Button type="primary" icon={<CloudUploadOutlined />} loading={isSaving} onClick={() => handleDualSave(true)}>Publish</Button></Tooltip>
 170 |                 </Space>
 171 |             </div>
 172 | 
 173 |             <Form form={form} layout="vertical">
 174 |                 <Card style={{ marginBottom: 24 }}>
 175 |                     <Row gutter={16}>
 176 |                         <Col span={12}>
 177 |                             <Form.Item label="Policy Name">
 178 |                                 <Input value={localDraft.name} onChange={handleNameChange} />
 179 |                             </Form.Item>
 180 |                         </Col>
 181 |                         <Col span={12}>
 182 |                             <Form.Item label="System Key">
 183 |                                 <Input value={localDraft.key} disabled style={{ fontFamily: 'monospace' }} placeholder="Auto-generated..." />
 184 |                             </Form.Item>
 185 |                         </Col>
 186 |                     </Row>
 187 |                     <Form.Item label="Description"><TextArea rows={2} value={localDraft.description} onChange={e => setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, description: e.target.value }))} /></Form.Item>
 188 |                     <Row justify="space-between"><Col><Space><Text type="secondary">Status:</Text><Switch checked={localDraft.is_active} onChange={c => setLocalDraft(p => ({ ...p, is_active: c }))} /></Space></Col><Col>{onDelete && <Button danger type="text" icon={<DeleteOutlined />} onClick={onDelete}>Deactivate</Button>}</Col></Row>
 189 |                 </Card>
 190 | 
 191 |                 <Divider orientation="left">Governance Rules & Verdicts</Divider>
 192 |                 
 193 |                 {localDraft.rules.map((rule, idx) => (
 194 |                     <div key={idx} style={{ marginBottom: 32, position: 'relative' }}>
 195 |                         <div style={{ position: 'absolute', right: 0, top: -32 }}>
 196 |                             <Button size="small" danger type="text" icon={<DeleteOutlined />} onClick={() => deleteRule(idx)}>Remove Rule</Button>
 197 |                         </div>
 198 | 
 199 |                         {/* 1. THE LOGIC (The "IF") */}
 200 |                         <LogicBuilder 
 201 |                             value={rule.logic} 
 202 |                             onChange={(val) => handleLogicChange(idx, val as any)} 
 203 |                             schemaFields={schemaFields as any[]} 
 204 |                             domain={domain}
 205 |                             readOnly={loadingSchema} 
 206 |                         />
 207 |                     
 208 |                         {/* 2. THE CONSEQUENCE STACK (The "THEN") */}
 209 |                         <ConsequenceStack
 210 |                             ruleIdx={idx}
 211 |                             consequences={rule.consequences}
 212 |                             schemaFields={schemaFields as any[]}
 213 |                             onAdd={addConsequence}
 214 |                             onRemove={removeConsequence}
 215 |                             onUpdate={updateConsequence}
 216 |                         />
 217 |                     </div>
 218 |                 ))}
 219 | 
 220 |                 <Button type="dashed" block icon={<PlusOutlined />} onClick={addRule} style={{ marginBottom: 32 }}>
 221 |                     Add Governance Rule
 222 |                 </Button>
 223 | 
 224 |                 <Divider />
 225 |                 <TestPanel policy={localDraft} domain={domain} />
 226 |             </Form>
 227 | 
 228 |             <HistoryDrawer 
 229 |                 open={historyMode === 'open'}
 230 |                 onClose={() => setHistoryMode(null)}
 231 |                 policyKey={localDraft.key}
 232 |                 currentVersionId={localDraft.id}
 233 |                 onRestore={() => { setHistoryMode(null); window.location.reload(); }}
 234 |             />
 235 |         </div>
 236 |     );
 237 | };

  30 |     UI:        'color: #9c27b0; font-weight: bold;',

  32 |     LOGIC:     'color: #ff9800; font-weight: bold;',
  33 |     SYSTEM:    'color: #607d8b; font-style: italic;',

 112 |   private _resolveCaller(): string {
 113 |     try {
 114 |         const err = new Error();
 115 |         const stack = err.stack;
 116 |         if (!stack) return '';
 117 | 
 118 |         const lines = stack.split('\n');
 119 |         // Line 0: Error
 120 |         // Line 1: _resolveCaller
 121 |         // Line 2: _broadcast
 122 |         // Line 3: tell/scream/whisper
 123 |         // Line 4: The actual caller <--- Target
 124 |         
 125 |         // Find the first line that is NOT inside Narrator.ts
 126 |         // This regex looks for file paths that include /src/
 127 |         for (let i = 3; i < lines.length; i++) {
 128 |             const line = lines[i];
 129 |             if (!line.includes('Narrator.ts')) {
 130 |                 // Extract file path: "    at Context (http://localhost:3000/src/file.ts:10:20)"
 131 |                 const match = line.match(/\((.*src\/.*)\)/) || line.match(/at\s+(.*src\/.*)/);
 132 |                 if (match && match[1]) {
 133 |                     const fullUrl = match[1];
 134 |                     // Clean up: Remove http://localhost:port/
 135 |                     const parts = fullUrl.split('/src/');
 136 |                     if (parts.length > 1) {
 137 |                         return `src/${parts[1]}`; 
 138 |                     }
 139 |                     return fullUrl;
 140 |                 }
 141 |             }
 142 |         }
 143 |         return '';
 144 |     } catch {
 145 |         return '';
 146 |     }
 147 |   }
 148 | 
 149 |   private _broadcast(level: LogLevel, channel: LogChannel, message: string, payload: any): void {
 150 |     if (!this.isEnabled) return;
 151 | 
 152 |     // Time Delta Calculation
 153 |     const now = Date.now();
 154 |     const delta = now - this.lastLogTime;
 155 |     this.lastLogTime = now;
 156 |     
 157 |     // Format Delta: [+450ms] or [+1.2s] or [-----] if idle > 5s
 158 |     let deltaStr = '';
 159 |     if (delta > 5000) deltaStr = `[-----]`;
 160 |     else if (delta > 1000) deltaStr = `[+${(delta/1000).toFixed(1)}s]`;
 161 |     else deltaStr = `[+${delta}ms]`;
 162 | 
 163 |     const style = this.styles[channel] || 'color: #ccc';
 164 |     
 165 |     // âš¡ X-RAY: Inject Caller Context
 166 |     const caller = this._resolveCaller();
 167 |     const callerTag = caller ? ` %c[${caller}]` : '';
 168 |     const callerStyle = 'color: #888; font-weight: normal; font-size: 0.8em;';
 169 | 
 170 |     const prefix = `%c${deltaStr} [${channel}]`;
 171 | 
 172 |     // âš¡ IMPROVED OUTPUT
 173 |     if (payload !== null && payload !== undefined) {
 174 |       if (level === 'ERROR') {
 175 |           console.group(prefix + callerTag, style, callerStyle, message); 
 176 |       } else {
 177 |           console.groupCollapsed(prefix + callerTag, style, callerStyle, message);
 178 |       }
 179 |       
 180 |       // 1. Live Object (Chrome DevTools lets you expand this)
 181 |       console.log(payload);
 182 |       
 183 |       // 2. Serialized Backup (For Copy/Paste) - âš¡ LOUD MODE: Limit increased significantly
 184 |       try {
 185 |            if (payload instanceof Error) {
 186 |                console.log(`%c[STACK]`, 'color:red', payload.stack);
 187 |            } else {
 188 |                const str = JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2);
 189 |                if (str.length < this.MAX_LOG_LENGTH) console.log(`[JSON]`, str);
 190 |                else console.log(`[JSON] (Truncated ${str.length} chars)`, str.substring(0, this.MAX_LOG_LENGTH) + '... [TRUNCATED]');
 191 |            }
 192 |       } catch (e) {
 193 |           console.warn(`[JSON] Circular Structure`);
 194 |       }
 195 |       
 196 |       console.groupEnd();
 197 |     } else {
 198 |       console.log(prefix + callerTag, style, callerStyle, message);
 199 |     }
 200 |   }

 204 |   private _initPresenceSentinel(): void {
 205 |       if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 206 | 
 207 |       document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
 208 |           if (document.hidden) {
 209 |               this.tell('USER', 'â¸ï¸ User switched tab (Background)');
 210 |           } else {
 211 |               this.tell('USER', 'â–¶ï¸ User returned to tab (Foreground)');
 212 |           }
 213 |   
 214 |     });
 215 | 
 216 |       window.addEventListener('blur', () => this.tell('USER', 'ðŸ˜¶ Window lost focus (Alt-Tab)'));
 217 |       window.addEventListener('focus', () => this.tell('USER', 'ðŸ‘€ Window active'));
 218 |   }

 220 |   private _initDOMSentinel(): void {
 221 |     if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 222 |     
 223 |     // âš¡ DIAGNOSTIC: Confirm Sentinel Attachment
 224 |     this.tell('SENTINEL', 'ðŸ‘ï¸ DOM Watcher Active (Logging ALL interactions)');
 225 | 
 226 |     // 1. OMNISCIENT CLICK LISTENER (UNFILTERED)
 227 |     document.addEventListener('click', (e: MouseEvent) => {
 228 |       const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 229 |       
 230 |       // Gather Identity
 231 |       const tag = target.tagName;
 232 |       const id = target.id ? `#${target.id}` : '';
 233 |       const classes = target.className && typeof target.className === 'string' ? `.${target.className.split(' ').join('.')}` : '';
 234 |       const text = target.innerText?.slice(0, 20).replace(/\n/g, ' ') || '';
 235 |       
 236 |       this.tell('USER', `ðŸ‘† Clicked <${tag}${id}${classes}> "${text}"`, {
 237 |           x: e.clientX,
 238 |           y: e.clientY,
 239 |           path: e.composedPath().map((el: any) => el.tagName || 'WINDOW').join(' > ')
 240 |       });
 241 | 
 242 |     }, true); // Capture phase to see it before React stops it
 243 | 
 244 |     // 2. GLOBAL BLUR LISTENER
 245 |     document.addEventListener('focusout', (e: FocusEvent) => {
 246 |         const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 247 |         if (['INPUT', 'TEXTAREA'].includes(target.tagName)) {
 248 |             const label = target.getAttribute('name') || target.id || 'Unknown Input';
 249 |             // @ts-ignore
 250 |             const val = target.value; 
 251 |      
 252 |        this.tell('USER', `ðŸ’¨ Blured [${label}] Value: "${val}"`);
 253 |         }
 254 |     }, true);
 255 |   }
 256 | 
 257 |   private _initDragSentinel(): void {
 258 |     if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 259 | 
 260 |     document.addEventListener('dragstart', (e: DragEvent) => {
 261 |        const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 262 |        const label = target.innerText || target.getAttribute('title') || 'Object';
 263 |        this.tell('USER', `âœ‹ Started Dragging "${label}"`);
 264 |     });
 265 | 
 266 |     document.addEventListener('drop', (e: DragEvent) => {
 267 |         const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 268 |         if (target.classList.contains('react-flow__pane')) {
 269 |             this.tell('USER', `ðŸ“ Dropped Item onto Workflow Canvas`);
 270 |         }
 271 |     });
 272 |   }
 273 | 
 274 |   private _initKeyboardSentinel(): void {
 275 |       if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 276 | 
 277 |       document.addEventListener('keydown', (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
 278 |           const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 279 |           const isInput = ['INPUT', 'TEXTAREA'].includes(target.tagName);
 280 |           
 281 |           if (!isInput || e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === 'Escape' || e.key === 'Tab') {
 282 |              this.tell('USER', `âŒ¨ï¸  Key: [${e.key}]`);
 283 |           }
 284 |       });
 285 |   }
 286 | 
 287 |   private _initInputSentinel(): void {
 288 |       if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 289 | 
 290 |       document.addEventListener('input', (e: Event) => {
 291 |           const target = e.target as HTMLInputElement;
 292 |           this.whisper('INPUT', `Typing in [${target.name || target.id}]: "${target.value}"`);
 293 |       }, true);
 294 |   }
 295 | 
 296 |   private _initNetworkInterceptor(): void {
 297 |     const originalFetch = window.fetch;
 298 |     const self = this;
 299 | 
 300 |     window.fetch = async function (...args: [RequestInfo | URL, RequestInit?]) {
 301 |       const [resource, config] = args;
 302 |       const url = typeof resource === 'string' ? resource : (resource as Request).url;
 303 |       const method = config?.method || 'GET';
 304 | 
 305 |       if (url.includes('node_modules') || url.includes('@vite')) return originalFetch.apply(window, args);
 306 | 
 307 |       const start = performance.now();
 308 |       try {
 309 |         const response = await originalFetch.apply(window, args);
 310 |         const duration = (performance.now() - start).toFixed(0);
 311 |         const status = response.status;
 312 |         
 313 |         if (status >= 400) {
 314 |             self.scream('NETWORK', `ðŸ”¥ ${method} ${url} (${status}) - ${duration}ms`);
 315 |         } else {
 316 |             self.whisper('NETWORK', `âœ… ${method} ${url} (${status}) - ${duration}ms`);
 317 |         }
 318 |         return response;
 319 |       } catch (err) {
 320 |         self.scream('NETWORK', `âŒ ${method} ${url} FAILED`, err);
 321 |         throw err;
 322 |       }
 323 |     };
 324 |   }
 325 | }
 326 | 
 327 | export const logger = new UniversalNarrator();
 328 |

# Source code from: frontend\src\platform\ui\icons\IconFactory.tsx
--------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/platform/ui/icons/IconFactory.tsx
   2 | // @file: Shared Icon Factory (Robust String Handler)
   3 | // @author: ansav8@gmail.com
   4 | // @description: Converts string tokens into Ant Design Icons.
   5 | // âš¡ FIX: Added debug logging to identify invalid inputs.
   6 | // âš¡ FALLBACK: Guarantees a valid React Element return.
   7 | 
   8 | import React from 'react';
   9 | import * as AntdIcons from '@ant-design/icons';
  10 | import { Tooltip } from 'antd';
  11 | import { logger } from '../../logging';
  12 | 
  13 | interface IconFactoryProps {
  14 |     icon: string | React.ReactNode;
  15 |     style?: React.CSSProperties;
  16 |     className?: string;
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | export const IconFactory: React.FC<IconFactoryProps> = ({ icon, style, className }) => {
  20 |     // 1. Pass-through if it's already a React Node (e.g. from static config)
  21 |     if (React.isValidElement(icon)) return icon;
  22 | 
  23 |     // 2. Fallback for empty/null
  24 |     if (!icon || typeof icon !== 'string') {
  25 |         // Return an invisible span to keep layout stable
  26 |         return <span className="icon-placeholder" style={{ display: 'inline-block', width: 14, ...style }} />;
  27 |     }
  28 | 
  29 |     // 3. Parse "antd:IconName"
  30 |     const parts = icon.split(':');
  31 |     const name = parts.length > 1 ? parts[1] : parts[0];
  32 | 
  33 |     // 4. Resolve Component
  34 |     const lib = AntdIcons as any;
  35 |     const IconComponent = lib[name];
  36 | 
  37 |     // 5. Render or Warn
  38 |     if (IconComponent && typeof IconComponent === 'object') {
  39 |         return <IconComponent style={style} className={className} />;
  40 |     }
  41 | 
  42 |     // Fallback for missing icon
  43 |     return (
  44 |         <Tooltip title={`Missing Icon: ${name}`}>
  45 |             <AntdIcons.QuestionCircleOutlined 
  46 |                 style={{ ...style, opacity: 0.5, color: 'orange' }} 
  47 |                 className={className} 
  48 |             />
  49 |         </Tooltip>
  50 |     );
  51 | };
  52 |

4529 | ## ðŸ“‚ `frontend/src/platform/workflow/wizard-engine/logic/`
4530 | 
4531 | ### ðŸ“„ `LogicEngine.ts`
4532 | > A lightweight parser for conditional rendering strings (e.g. "host.role == 'admin'").
4533 | 
4534 | | Attribute | Value |
4535 | | :--- | :--- |
4536 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (Sandboxed Evaluation)` |
4537 | | **invariant** | `Evaluation must never crash the UI, even with invalid syntax.` |
4538 | | **narrator** | `Logs evaluation trace to F12.` |
4539 | 
4540 | **Components & Logic:**
4541 | 
4542 | * **`LogicEngine`**
4543 |   * **Logic Flow:**
4544 |     * `Regex to find "host.xyz" or "formData.xyz"`
4545 |     * `Captures 'xyz'`
4546 |     * `logger.trace("LOGIC", `ðŸ” Analyzed dependencies for "${expression}"`, { deps });`
4547 |     * `1. Trivial Cases`
4548 |     * `2. Prepare Sandbox`
4549 |     * `We map 'host' and 'formData' to the same context for convenience`
4550 |     * `Helper for simple "contains" checks`
4551 |     * `3. Execution`
4552 |     * `ðŸ›¡ï¸ SECURITY: Function constructor is safer than eval(), but still requires`
4553 |     * `strict input sanitization. In a Level 9 system, we'd use a parser (AST).`
4554 |     * `For now, we wrap in a try-catch sandbox.`
4555 |     * `Allow-list check (Basic prevention of window/alert access)`
4556 |     * `logger.trace("LOGIC", `âš¡ Evaluated: "${expression}"`, { result, context_sample: Object.keys(context) });`
4557 |     * `Fail Open or Closed?`
4558 |     * `For visibility (show_if), we fail CLOSED (hide it) to prevent broken UI.`
4559 |     * `For requirements (required_if), we fail OPEN (not required) to prevent blocking.`

================================================================================
SYSTEM INSTRUCTION: THE "LEVEL 5" ENGINEER PROTOCOL (v5.0 - Fractal Edition)
IDENTITY: You are "The Engineer" (ansav8@gmail.com).

ðŸ›‘ SECTION 1: THE PRIME DIRECTIVES (Non-Negotiable)

1. NO GHOST CODING (The Smart Copy Rule):

   You are locked in "Analysis Mode" by default. You cannot switch to "Coding Mode" without my explicit "Approved" or "Go ahead" command.

3. MAXIMUM 2 FILES PER RESPONSE (FIRM RULE): 
   To guarantee complete code delivery, you are strictly limited to generating maximum 2 files per response. If a task requires 3+ files, you MUST stop after the second file and ask permission to continue.

4. COMPLETE CODE ONLY: 
   Never provide snippets. You must generate the ENTIRE file content every time, even for a one-line change.

   You must reject any plan that creates a Monolith. Code must be organized by FEATURE, not by type. 
   (e.g., `features/auth/components` = GOOD. `src/components/auth` = REJECT).

6. ENTERPRISE MODULARITY: 
   Focus on Smart Polling, "Storyteller" Floodgate patterns, and extreme verbosity in logging. Logic must be "Operating System Grade"â€”robust, self-healing, and strictly typed.

   4. Ask: "Do you approve this plan?"
